    25→/* ===== State ===== */
    26→let recognition     = null;
    27→let isListening     = false;
    28→let activeMode      = null; // 'quick' | 'brainstorm' | null
    29→let finalTranscript = '';
    30→let interimText     = '';
    31→let silenceTimer    = null;
    32→const SILENCE_DELAY = 3500; // ms — only used in quick mode
    33→
    34→/* ===== Brainstorm continuity ===== */
    35→// Chrome stops continuous recognition periodically; we restart seamlessly in brainstorm mode
    36→// and preserve accumulated transcript across restarts.
    37→let brainstormAccumulator  = '';
    38→let _brainstormRestarting  = false;
    39→
    40→/* ===== Wake word state ===== */
    41→let wakeRecognition       = null;
    42→let wakeMode              = false;
    43→let wakeTriggered         = false; // transitioning from wake → main recording
    44→let wakeTriggeredRecording = false; // current recording was initiated by wake word
    45→let wakeRestartTimer      = null;
    46→const WAKE_PHRASES        = ['hey chill', 'hey chil']; // core phrase + common partial
    47→
    48→/* ===== Audio Feedback ===== */
    49→let audioCtx = null;
    50→
    51→function getAudioContext() {
    52→  if (!audioCtx) {
    53→    audioCtx = new (window.AudioContext || window.webkitAudioContext)();
    54→  }
    55→  if (audioCtx.state === 'suspended') {
    56→    audioCtx.resume();
    57→  }
    58→  return audioCtx;
    59→}
    60→
    61→// Prime the AudioContext on first user interaction so it's ready for hands-free sends
    62→function primeAudio() {
    63→  try { getAudioContext(); } catch (_) {}
    64→}
    65→
    66→function _playTone(ctx, frequency, startTime, duration, gain) {
    67→  const osc  = ctx.createOscillator();
    68→  const amp  = ctx.createGain();
    69→  osc.connect(amp);
    70→  amp.connect(ctx.destination);
    71→  osc.type = 'sine';
    72→  osc.frequency.setValueAtTime(frequency, startTime);
    73→  amp.gain.setValueAtTime(0, startTime);
    74→  amp.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(gain, startTime + 0.01);
    75→  amp.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.001, startTime + duration);
    76→  osc.start(startTime);
    77→  osc.stop(startTime + duration);
    78→}
    79→
    80→function playSuccessSound() {
    81→  // Prefer speech synthesis — "Got it" is immediately understood
    82→  if ('speechSynthesis' in window) {
    83→    const utt = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance('Got it');
    84→    utt.rate   = 1.1;
    85→    utt.pitch  = 1.1;
    86→    utt.volume = 1;
    87→    window.speechSynthesis.speak(utt);
    88→    return;
    89→  }
    90→  // Fallback: ascending double chime
    91→  try {
    92→    const ctx = getAudioContext();
    93→    const now = ctx.currentTime;
    94→    _playTone(ctx, 880,  now,        0.22, 0.30); // A5
    95→    _playTone(ctx, 1320, now + 0.18, 0.38, 0.25); // E6
    96→  } catch (e) {
    97→    console.warn('Audio playback failed:', e);
    98→  }
    99→}
   100→
   101→function playFailureSound() {
   102→  // Descending dissonant triple-tone — distinct "uh-oh" signal
   103→  try {
   104→    const ctx = getAudioContext();
   105→    const now = ctx.currentTime;
   106→    _playTone(ctx, 330, now,        0.18, 0.40); // E4
   107→    _playTone(ctx, 262, now + 0.15, 0.18, 0.40); // C4
   108→    _playTone(ctx, 196, now + 0.30, 0.45, 0.35); // G3
   109→  } catch (e) {
   110→    console.warn('Audio playback failed:', e);
   111→  }
   112→}
   113→
   114→/* ===== Service Worker ===== */
   115→if ('serviceWorker' in navigator) {
   116→  navigator.serviceWorker.register('sw.js').catch(() => {/* silent */});
   117→}
   118→
   119→/* ===== Speech Recognition setup ===== */
   120→const SpeechRecognition = window.SpeechRecognition || window.webkitSpeechRecognition;
   121→
   122→if (!SpeechRecognition) {
   123→  notSupported.hidden = false;
   124→  quickBtn.disabled = true;
   125→  quickBtn.setAttribute('aria-disabled', 'true');
   126→  brainstormBtn.disabled = true;
   127→  brainstormBtn.setAttribute('aria-disabled', 'true');
   128→} else {
   129→  initRecognition();
   130→}
   131→
   132→function initRecognition() {
   133→  recognition = new SpeechRecognition();
   134→  recognition.continuous     = true;
   135→  recognition.interimResults = true;
   136→  recognition.lang           = navigator.language || 'en-US';
   137→  recognition.maxAlternatives = 1;
   138→
   139→  recognition.onstart = () => {
   140→    if (_brainstormRestarting) {
   141→      // Seamless brainstorm restart — preserve accumulated transcript, don't reset UI
   142→      isListening = true;
   143→      finalTranscript = brainstormAccumulator;
   144→      interimText = '';
   145→      _brainstormRestarting = false;
   146→      return;
   147→    }
   148→    isListening = true;
   149→    finalTranscript = '';
   150→    brainstormAccumulator = '';
   151→    interimText = '';
   152→    setRecordingUI(true, activeMode);
   153→  };
   154→
   155→  recognition.onresult = (event) => {
   156→    let interim = '';
   157→    for (let i = event.resultIndex; i < event.results.length; i++) {
   158→      const result = event.results[i];
   159→      if (result.isFinal) {
   160→        finalTranscript += result[0].transcript + ' ';
   161→      } else {
   162→        interim += result[0].transcript;
   163→      }
   164→    }
   165→    interimText = interim;
   166→    const displayText = (finalTranscript + interim).trim();
   167→    updateLiveText(displayText);
   168→
   169→    // Silence timer only applies to quick mode
   170→    if (activeMode === 'quick') {
   171→      resetSilenceTimer();
   172→    }
   173→  };
   174→
   175→  recognition.onerror = (event) => {
   176→    // 'no-speech' is common and expected — just stop cleanly
   177→    if (event.error !== 'no-speech') {
   178→      console.warn('Speech recognition error:', event.error);
   179→    }
   180→    _brainstormRestarting = false;
   181→    stopListening();
   182→  };
   183→
   184→  recognition.onend = () => {
   185→    if (isListening && activeMode === 'brainstorm') {
   186→      // Chrome stops continuous recognition periodically — restart seamlessly
   187→      brainstormAccumulator = finalTranscript;
   188→      _brainstormRestarting = true;
   189→      setTimeout(() => {
   190→        if (isListening && activeMode === 'brainstorm') {
   191→          try {
   192→            recognition.start();
   193→          } catch (_) {
   194→            _brainstormRestarting = false;
   195→            brainstormAccumulator = '';
   196→            isListening = false;
   197→            finishRecording();
   198→          }
   199→        } else {
   200→          _brainstormRestarting = false;
   201→        }
   202→      }, 150);
   203→      return;
   204→    }
   205→    // onend fires when recognition stops for any reason
   206→    if (isListening) {
   207→      // We didn't call stop manually yet; auto-stop happened
   208→      finishRecording();
   209→    }
   210→  };
   211→}
   212→
   213→function resetSilenceTimer() {
   214→  clearTimeout(silenceTimer);
   215→  silenceTimer = setTimeout(() => {
   216→    if (isListening) stopListening();
   217→  }, SILENCE_DELAY);
   218→}
   219→
   220→/* ===== Recording controls ===== */
   221→function startListening(mode) {
   222→  if (!recognition || isListening) return;
   223→  activeMode = mode;
   224→  hideTranscriptBar();
   225→
   226→  // Ensure wake recognition is stopped before starting main recording
   227→  if (wakeMode) stopWakeRecognition();
   228→
   229→  try {
   230→    recognition.start();
   231→  } catch (e) {
   232→    console.warn('Could not start recognition:', e);
   233→    // Re-init in case of invalid state
   234→    initRecognition();
   235→    try { recognition.start(); } catch (_) {}
   236→  }
   237→
   238→  if (mode === 'quick') {
   239→    resetSilenceTimer();
   240→  }
   241→}
   242→
   243→function stopListening() {
   244→  clearTimeout(silenceTimer);
   245→  _brainstormRestarting = false; // prevent auto-restart in brainstorm
   246→  isListening = false; // mark before calling stop so onend doesn't re-trigger finishRecording
   247→  if (recognition) {
   248→    try { recognition.stop(); } catch (_) {}
   249→  }
   250→  finishRecording();
   251→}
   252→
   253→function finishRecording() {
   254→  const mode = activeMode;
   255→  setRecordingUI(false, mode);
   256→  const text = finalTranscript.trim();
   257→  brainstormAccumulator = '';
   258→  activeMode = null;
   259→  if (text) {
   260→    if (wakeTriggeredRecording) {
   261→      // Hands-free path: auto-send without requiring a tap
   262→      sendMessage(text);
   263→    } else {
   264→      showTranscriptBar(text);
   265→    }
   266→  }
   267→  wakeTriggeredRecording = false;
   268→  // Resume passive wake word listening if mode is active
   269→  if (wakeMode) scheduleWakeRestart();
   270→  updateWakeHint();
   271→}
   272→
   273→/* ===== UI state helpers ===== */
   274→function setRecordingUI(recording, mode) {
   275→  const quickActive      = recording && mode === 'quick';
   276→  const brainstormActive = recording && mode === 'brainstorm';
   277→
   278→  // Quick button
   279→  quickBtn.classList.toggle('recording', quickActive);
   280→  quickRing.classList.toggle('recording', quickActive);
   281→  quickBtn.setAttribute('aria-pressed', quickActive ? 'true' : 'false');
   282→  quickBtn.setAttribute('aria-label', quickActive ? 'Stop recording' : 'Quick Request – tap to speak');
   283→
   284→  // Brainstorm button
   285→  brainstormBtn.classList.toggle('recording', brainstormActive);
   286→  brainstormRing.classList.toggle('recording', brainstormActive);
   287→  brainstormBtn.setAttribute('aria-pressed', brainstormActive ? 'true' : 'false');
   288→  brainstormBtn.setAttribute('aria-label', brainstormActive ? 'Stop brainstorm recording' : 'Brainstorm – tap for continuous recording');
   289→
   290→  // Shared hint
   291→  if (quickActive) {
   292→    micHint.textContent = 'Listening… tap Quick to stop';
   293→    micHint.classList.add('active');
   294→    micHint.classList.remove('brainstorm-active');
   295→  } else if (brainstormActive) {
   296→    micHint.textContent = 'Recording… tap Brainstorm to stop';
   297→    micHint.classList.add('active', 'brainstorm-active');
   298→  } else {
   299→    micHint.classList.remove('active', 'brainstorm-active');
   300→    updateWakeHint();
   301→  }
   302→
   303→  liveTranscript.hidden = !recording;
   304→  if (!recording) {
   305→    liveText.textContent = 'Listening…';
   306→    liveText.classList.remove('has-text');
   307→  }
   308→}
   309→
   310→function updateLiveText(text) {
   311→  if (text) {
   312→    liveText.textContent = text;
   313→    liveText.classList.add('has-text');
   314→  } else {
   315→    liveText.textContent = 'Listening…';
   316→    liveText.classList.remove('has-text');
   317→  }
   318→}
   319→
   320→function showTranscriptBar(text) {
   321→  transcriptText.textContent = text;
   322→  transcriptBar.hidden = false;
   323→}
   324→
   325→function hideTranscriptBar() {
   326→  transcriptBar.hidden = true;
   327→  transcriptText.textContent = '';
   328→}
   329→
   330→/* ===== Button click handlers ===== */
   331→quickBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
   332→  primeAudio();
   333→  if (isListening && activeMode === 'quick') {
   334→    stopListening();
   335→  } else if (!isListening) {
   336→    wakeTriggeredRecording = false; // manual tap — show transcript bar after
   337→    startListening('quick');
   338→  }
   339→});
   340→
   341→brainstormBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
   342→  primeAudio();
   343→  if (isListening && activeMode === 'brainstorm') {
   344→    stopListening();
   345→  } else if (!isListening) {
   346→    wakeTriggeredRecording = false;
   347→    startListening('brainstorm');
   348→  }
   349→});
   350→
   351→/* ===== Send / Discard ===== */
   352→sendBtn.addEventListener('click', async () => {
   353→  primeAudio();
   354→  const text = transcriptText.textContent.trim();
   355→  if (!text) return;
   356→  hideTranscriptBar();
   357→  await sendMessage(text);
   358→});
   359→
   360→discardBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
   361→  hideTranscriptBar();
   362→});
   363→
   364→/* ===== Webhook send ===== */
   365→async function sendMessage(text) {
   366→  const webhookUrl = localStorage.getItem('webhookUrl') || '';
   367→  const timestamp  = new Date().toISOString();
   368→  const payload    = { text, source: 'hey-chill', timestamp };
   369→
   370→  // Add message to history immediately
   371→  const msgEl = addMessage(text, timestamp, 'sending');
   372→
   373→  if (!webhookUrl) {
   374→    updateMessageStatus(msgEl, 'no-webhook');
   375→    return;
   376→  }
   377→
   378→  try {
   379→    const res = await fetch(webhookUrl, {
   380→      method: 'POST',
   381→      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
   382→      body: JSON.stringify(payload),
   383→    });
   384→    if (!res.ok) throw new Error(`HTTP ${res.status}`);
   385→    updateMessageStatus(msgEl, 'sent');
   386→    playSuccessSound();
   387→  } catch (err) {
   388→    console.warn('Webhook error:', err);
   389→    updateMessageStatus(msgEl, 'error');
   390→    playFailureSound();
   391→  }
   392→}
   393→
   394→/* ===== Message history ===== */
   395→function addMessage(text, timestamp, status) {
   396→  // Hide empty state
   397→  messagesEmpty.style.display = 'none';
   398→
   399→  const el = document.createElement('div');
   400→  el.className = `message ${status}`;
   401→
   402→  const timeStr = new Date(timestamp).toLocaleTimeString([], {
   403→    hour: '2-digit',
   404→    minute: '2-digit',
   405→  });
   406→
   407→  const statusLabel = {
   408→    sending:    'Sending…',
   409→    sent:       'Sent',
   410→    error:      'Failed',
   411→    'no-webhook': 'No webhook',
   412→  };
   413→
   414→  el.innerHTML = `
   415→    <p class="message-text">${escapeHtml(text)}</p>
   416→    <div class="message-meta">
   417→      <span class="message-time">${timeStr}</span>
   418→      <span class="message-status">${statusLabel[status] || status}</span>
   419→    </div>
   420→  `;
   421→
   422→  messagesEl.appendChild(el);
   423→  el.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'end' });
   424→  return el;
   425→}
   426→
   427→function updateMessageStatus(el, status) {
   428→  el.className = `message ${status}`;
   429→  const statusEl = el.querySelector('.message-status');
   430→  const labels = {
   431→    sent:         'Sent',
   432→    error:        'Failed',
   433→    'no-webhook': 'No webhook set',
   434→  };
   435→  if (statusEl) statusEl.textContent = labels[status] || status;
   436→}
   437→
   438→function escapeHtml(str) {
   439→  return str
   440→    .replace(/&/g, '&amp;')
   441→    .replace(/</g, '&lt;')
   442→    .replace(/>/g, '&gt;')
   443→    .replace(/"/g, '&quot;')
   444→    .replace(/'/g, '&#39;');
   445→}
   446→
   447→/* ===== Settings modal ===== */
   448→settingsBtn.addEventListener('click', openSettings);
   449→modalClose.addEventListener('click',  closeSettings);
   450→modalOverlay.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
   451→  if (e.target === modalOverlay) closeSettings();
   452→});
   453→
   454→document.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
   455→  if (e.key === 'Escape') closeSettings();
   456→});
   457→
   458→saveSettings.addEventListener('click', () => {
   459→  const url = webhookInput.value.trim();
   460→  localStorage.setItem('webhookUrl', url);
   461→  closeSettings();
   462→});
   463→
   464→function openSettings() {
   465→  webhookInput.value = localStorage.getItem('webhookUrl') || '';
   466→  modalOverlay.hidden = false;
   467→  webhookInput.focus();
   468→}
   469→
   470→function closeSettings() {
   471→  modalOverlay.hidden = true;
   472→}
   473→
   474→/* ===== Wake Word Detection ===== */
   475→
   476→function isWakePhrase(transcript) {
   477→  return WAKE_PHRASES.some(phrase => transcript.includes(phrase));
   478→}
   479→
   480→function initWakeRecognition() {
   481→  wakeRecognition = new SpeechRecognition();
   482→  wakeRecognition.continuous     = true;
   483→  wakeRecognition.interimResults = true;
   484→  wakeRecognition.lang           = navigator.language || 'en-US';
   485→  wakeRecognition.maxAlternatives = 1;
   486→
   487→  wakeRecognition.onresult = (event) => {
   488→    for (let i = event.resultIndex; i < event.results.length; i++) {
   489→      const transcript = event.results[i][0].transcript.toLowerCase().trim();
   490→      if (isWakePhrase(transcript)) {
   491→        handleWakeWordDetected();
   492→        return;
   493→      }
   494→    }
   495→  };
   496→
   497→  wakeRecognition.onerror = (event) => {
   498→    if (event.error === 'not-allowed' || event.error === 'service-not-allowed') {
   499→      // Microphone access denied — silently disable wake mode
   500→      disableWakeMode();
   501→      return;
   502→    }
   503→    if (wakeMode && !isListening && !wakeTriggered) {
   504→      scheduleWakeRestart();
   505→    }
   506→  };
   507→
   508→  wakeRecognition.onend = () => {
   509→    // Chrome stops continuous recognition periodically — restart unless we
   510→    // deliberately stopped it to hand off to main recording.
   511→    if (wakeMode && !isListening && !wakeTriggered) {
   512→      scheduleWakeRestart();
   513→    }
   514→  };
   515→}
   516→
   517→function startWakeRecognition() {
   518→  if (!wakeRecognition) initWakeRecognition();
   519→  wakeTriggered = false;
   520→  quickRing.classList.add('listening-passive'); // passive glow on quick button only
   521→  try {
   522→    wakeRecognition.start();
   523→  } catch (e) {
   524→    // InvalidStateError when already started — reinit and retry
   525→    initWakeRecognition();
   526→    try { wakeRecognition.start(); } catch (_) {}
   527→  }
   528→}
   529→
   530→function stopWakeRecognition() {
   531→  quickRing.classList.remove('listening-passive');
   532→  if (wakeRecognition) {
   533→    try { wakeRecognition.stop(); } catch (_) {}
   534→  }
   535→}
   536→
   537→function scheduleWakeRestart() {
   538→  clearTimeout(wakeRestartTimer);
   539→  wakeRestartTimer = setTimeout(() => {
   540→    if (wakeMode && !isListening && !wakeTriggered) {
   541→      startWakeRecognition();
   542→    }
   543→  }, 300);
   544→}
   545→
   546→function handleWakeWordDetected() {
   547→  if (isListening || wakeTriggered) return;
   548→  wakeTriggered = true;
   549→  wakeTriggeredRecording = true; // flag so finishRecording auto-sends
   550→  stopWakeRecognition();
   551→  // Give the recognition engine a moment to fully stop before starting main recording
   552→  setTimeout(() => {
   553→    wakeTriggered = false;
   554→    startListening('quick'); // wake word always triggers quick mode
   555→  }, 250);
   556→}
   557→
   558→function enableWakeMode() {
   559→  wakeMode = true;
   560→  wakeBtn.classList.add('wake-active');
   561→  wakeBtn.setAttribute('aria-pressed', 'true');
   562→  wakeBtn.setAttribute('aria-label', 'Disable wake word');
   563→  wakeBtn.title = 'Wake word: ON';
   564→  localStorage.setItem('wakeMode', '1');
   565→  updateWakeHint();
   566→  if (!isListening) startWakeRecognition();
   567→}
   568→
   569→function disableWakeMode() {
   570→  wakeMode = false;
   571→  wakeBtn.classList.remove('wake-active');
   572→  wakeBtn.setAttribute('aria-pressed', 'false');
   573→  wakeBtn.setAttribute('aria-label', 'Enable wake word');
   574→  wakeBtn.title = 'Wake word: Hey Chill';
   575→  localStorage.setItem('wakeMode', '0');
   576→  clearTimeout(wakeRestartTimer);
   577→  stopWakeRecognition();
   578→  updateWakeHint();
   579→}
   580→
   581→function updateWakeHint() {
   582→  if (!isListening) {
   583→    micHint.textContent = wakeMode ? 'Say "Hey Chill" or tap Quick' : '';
   584→    micHint.classList.remove('active', 'brainstorm-active');
   585→  }
   586→}
   587→
   588→wakeBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
   589→  primeAudio();
   590→  if (wakeMode) {
   591→    disableWakeMode();
   592→  } else {
   593→    enableWakeMode();
   594→  }
   595→});
   596→
   597→// Restore wake mode preference across sessions
   598→if (SpeechRecognition && localStorage.getItem('wakeMode') === '1') {
   599→  enableWakeMode();
   600→}
   601→

    50→  }
    51→

ASSISTANTMESSAGE #95
--- ## Status DONE ## What Changed - **`index.html`** — added `#transcript-cleaned-label` (label shown above cleaned text in brainstorm) and `#transcript-raw-wrap` / `#transcript-raw-text` (raw transcript section, hidden in quick mode) - **`style.css`** — added `.transcript-section-label`, `.transcript-raw-wrap`, `.transcript-raw-text` styles for the dual-transcript layout; added `.live-transcript.brainstorm-mode` for a 130 px max-height scrollable live transcript - **`app.js`** — new DOM refs for the three new elements; `cleanTranscript()` strips filler sounds (`um/uh/er/hmm`), fixes capitalisation, adds terminal period; `showTranscriptBar(text, mode)` now renders cleaned+raw sections in brainstorm, single section in quick; `hideTranscriptBar()` resets both; `setRecordingUI()` toggles `.brainstorm-mode` class; `updateLiveText()` auto-scrolls the live panel during brainstorm ## Key Decisions - **Send posts the cleaned version** — cleaned text goes into `#transcript-text` (what Send reads), raw is shown below as reference. This matches the "readable" intent without needing a second button. - **Conservative filler removal** — only obvious non-semantic sounds (`um/uh/er/hmm`) are stripped; content words like "actually" or "like" are preserved to avoid accidentally altering meaning. ## PR / Branch - Branch: `feature/frg-212-brainstorm-dual-transcript` - PR: https://github.com/chillkimtest-oss/hey-chill/pull/6
